Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: carbon\\ \tt RIGHT: pencils\\ \tt TOP: knife\\ \tt BOTTOM: mirror\\ \tt CENTER: lemon\\ \tt NORTHWEST: eraser\\ \tt NORTHEAST: highlighter\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: scissors\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: copper\\ \tt HERE: crayons\\ \tt THERE: iron\\ \tt NOWHERE: ukulele\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: ladder\\ \tt INSIDE: bucket\\ \tt OUTSIDE: post-it notes\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start. 
	  }

	   }

	  } 
	   } 
	   }
